# -------------------- utils.py (Folder: skills_output2\skills\451f2e7a\scripts) --------------------

def fibonacci(n, memo=None):
    """Calculate Fibonacci number using memoization."""
    # Check if the input is an integer
    if not isinstance(n, int):
        raise TypeError("Input must be an integer")
    
    # Handle negative input
    if n < 0:
        raise ValueError("Input cannot be negative")
    
    # Initialize memoization dictionary on the first call
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
    
    # Check if the result is already cached
    if n in memo:
        return memo[n]
    
    # Base cases
    if n == 0:
        return 0
    elif n == 1:
        return 1
    
    # Recursive relation
    memo[n] = fibonacci(n - 1, memo) + fibonacci(n - 2, memo)
    
    return memo[n]

# Alias for the fibonacci function for testing
solution = fibonacci

# Testing the implementation with various input values
if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_cases = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 10, 20]
    results = {n: solution(n) for n in test_cases}
    print(results)  # Outputs Fibonacci numbers for the test cases

# -------------------- utils.py (Folder: skills_output2\skills\4aeb6f33\scripts) --------------------

def fib(n, memo=None):
    # Initialize the memoization structure if not provided
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
    
    # Clear base cases
    if n in memo:
        return memo[n]
    if n == 0:
        return 0
    if n == 1:
        return 1
    
    # Recursive calculation with memoization
    memo[n] = fib(n-1, memo) + fib(n-2, memo)
    return memo[n]

# Testing the function with a variety of input cases
if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_cases = [0, 1, 5, 10, 20]
    for case in test_cases:
        print(f"Fibonacci({case}) = {fib(case)}")

    # Additional test cases for verification
    try:
        assert fib(0) == 0, "Test case 0 failed"
        assert fib(1) == 1, "Test case 1 failed"
        assert fib(5) == 5, "Test case 5 failed"
        assert fib(10) == 55, "Test case 10 failed"
        assert fib(20) == 6765, "Test case 20 failed"
        print("All test cases passed!")
    except AssertionError as e:
        print(e)

# -------------------- utils.py (Folder: skills_output2\skills\5173a4e3\scripts) --------------------

def fibonacci(n, memo=None):
    """
    Calculate the nth Fibonacci number using memoization.

    Args:
    n (int): The position in the Fibonacci sequence (non-negative integer).

    Returns:
    int: The nth Fibonacci number.

    Raises:
    ValueError: If n is a negative integer.
    """
    if n < 0:
        raise ValueError("Input must be a non-negative integer.")
    
    if memo is None:  # Initialize memo as a new dictionary if not provided
        memo = {}

    if n in memo:
        return memo[n]

    if n == 0:
        return 0
    elif n == 1:
        return 1

    memo[n] = fibonacci(n - 1, memo) + fibonacci(n - 2, memo)
    return memo[n]

# Test cases
def test_fibonacci_memoization():
    assert fibonacci(0) == 0, "Test case 0 failed"
    assert fibonacci(1) == 1, "Test case 1 failed"
    assert fibonacci(5) == 5, "Test case 5 failed"
    assert fibonacci(10) == 55, "Test case 10 failed"
    assert fibonacci(20) == 6765, "Test case 20 failed"
    print("All test cases passed!")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_fibonacci_memoization()

# -------------------- utils.py (Folder: skills_output2\skills\545fba2b\scripts) --------------------

def fibonacci(n, memo=None):
    # Initialize memoization dictionary if it's None
    if memo is None:
        memo = {}
    
    # Enforce base case handling
    if n < 0:
        raise ValueError("Input must be a non-negative integer.")
    if n in memo:
        return memo[n]
    if n == 0:
        return 0
    if n == 1:
        return 1
    
    # Calculate the Fibonacci number recursively and store it in memo
    result = fibonacci(n - 1, memo) + fibonacci(n - 2, memo)
    memo[n] = result
    return result

# Example test function

    assert fibonacci(0) == 0, "Test case 0 failed"

# -------------------- utils.py (Folder: skills_output2\skills\72c97f01\scripts) --------------------

def fibonacci(n, cache=None):
    # Handle negative inputs and non-integer inputs
    if not isinstance(n, int) or n < 0:
        raise ValueError("Input must be a non-negative integer.")
    
    # Initialize cache on the first call
    if cache is None:
        cache = {}
    
    # Base cases
    if n == 0:
        return 0
    if n == 1:
        return 1
    
    # Check if the result is already cached
    if n in cache:
        return cache[n]
    
    # Recursive calculation with memoization
    result = fibonacci(n - 1, cache) + fibonacci(n - 2, cache)
    
    # Store the result in cache
    cache[n] = result
    
    return result

# Testing the function with a range of inputs including a non-integer case
test_cases = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 10, 20, 5.5]
for n in test_cases:
    if not isinstance(n, int) or n < 0:
        print(f"Fibonacci({n}) is invalid: Input must be a non-negative integer.")
        continue
    try:
        print(f"Fibonacci({n}) = {fibonacci(n)}")
    except ValueError as e:
        print(f"Fibonacci({n}) raised a ValueError: {e}")

# -------------------- utils.py (Folder: skills_output2\skills\971ee7af\scripts) --------------------

def fibonacci(n):
    if n == 0:
        return 0
    if n == 1:
        return 1

    memo = {0: 0, 1: 1}
    for i in range(2, n + 1):
        memo[i] = memo[i - 1] + memo[i - 2]
    
    return memo[n]

# Testing the function with edge cases and typical scenarios
if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_cases = [0, 1, 2, 5, 10, 20, 30, 1000]
    results = {n: fibonacci(n) for n in test_cases}
    print(results)  # Expected output for other cases
    
    # Correct expected value for Fibonacci(1000)
    assert fibonacci(1000) == 703303677114202764, "Test case 1000 failed"  # Update the expected value if necessary

# -------------------- utils.py (Folder: skills_output2\skills\be1839fe\scripts) --------------------

def fibonacci(n, memo={}):
    """
    Calculate the n-th Fibonacci number using memoization.
    
    Parameters:
    n (int): The position in the Fibonacci sequence.
    memo (dict): A dictionary to store previously computed Fibonacci values.
    
    Returns:
    int: The n-th Fibonacci number.
    """
    # Handle negative inputs
    if n < 0:
        raise ValueError("Input should be a non-negative integer.")
    
    # Base cases
    if n in memo:
        return memo[n]  # Return the cached value if exists
    if n == 0:
        return 0
    if n == 1:
        return 1
    
    # Calculate the Fibonacci number recursively with memoization
    memo[n] = fibonacci(n - 1, memo) + fibonacci(n - 2, memo)
    return memo[n]

# Testing the implementation with various inputs
if __name__ == "__main__":
    test_cases = [0, 1, 5, 10, 15]
    for n in test_cases:
        print(f"F({n}) = {fibonacci(n)}")
